2024-02-14 21:17:55.677 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (19ms) [Parameters=[@__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32), @__p_1='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [t].[Name], [t].[Price], [t].[Stock], [t].[ID], [t0].[ID], [t0].[CreateTime], [t0].[Discriminator], [t0].[FileName], [t0].[Path], [t0].[Storage], [t0].[Showcase], [t0].[ProductImageFilesID], [t0].[ProductsID], [t].[CreateTime], [t].[UpdateTime]
FROM (
    SELECT [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Stock], [p].[ID], [p].[CreateTime], [p].[UpdateTime]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t1].[ID], [t1].[CreateTime], [t1].[Discriminator], [t1].[FileName], [t1].[Path], [t1].[Storage], [t1].[Showcase], [p0].[ProductImageFilesID], [p0].[ProductsID]
    FROM [ProductProductImageFile] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [f].[ID], [f].[CreateTime], [f].[Discriminator], [f].[FileName], [f].[Path], [f].[Storage], [f].[Showcase]
        FROM [Files] AS [f]
        WHERE [f].[Discriminator] = N'ProductImageFile'
    ) AS [t1] ON [p0].[ProductImageFilesID] = [t1].[ID]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ID] = [t0].[ProductsID]
ORDER BY [t].[ID], [t0].[ProductImageFilesID], [t0].[ProductsID]

2024-02-14 21:18:02.097 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (1ms) [Parameters=[@__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32), @__p_1='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [t].[Name], [t].[Price], [t].[Stock], [t].[ID], [t0].[ID], [t0].[CreateTime], [t0].[Discriminator], [t0].[FileName], [t0].[Path], [t0].[Storage], [t0].[Showcase], [t0].[ProductImageFilesID], [t0].[ProductsID], [t].[CreateTime], [t].[UpdateTime]
FROM (
    SELECT [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Stock], [p].[ID], [p].[CreateTime], [p].[UpdateTime]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t1].[ID], [t1].[CreateTime], [t1].[Discriminator], [t1].[FileName], [t1].[Path], [t1].[Storage], [t1].[Showcase], [p0].[ProductImageFilesID], [p0].[ProductsID]
    FROM [ProductProductImageFile] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [f].[ID], [f].[CreateTime], [f].[Discriminator], [f].[FileName], [f].[Path], [f].[Storage], [f].[Showcase]
        FROM [Files] AS [f]
        WHERE [f].[Discriminator] = N'ProductImageFile'
    ) AS [t1] ON [p0].[ProductImageFilesID] = [t1].[ID]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ID] = [t0].[ProductsID]
ORDER BY [t].[ID], [t0].[ProductImageFilesID], [t0].[ProductsID]
